\DoxyCodeLine{48                                          \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{49   \textcolor{comment}{// The calculation below is a static identity for unsigned types, but for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{50   \textcolor{comment}{// signed integer types it provides a non-\/branching, saturated absolute value.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{51   \textcolor{comment}{// This works because SafeUnsignedAbs() returns an unsigned type, which can}}
\DoxyCodeLine{52   \textcolor{comment}{// represent the absolute value of all negative numbers of an equal-\/width}}
\DoxyCodeLine{53   \textcolor{comment}{// integer type. The call to IsValueNegative() then detects overflow in the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{54   \textcolor{comment}{// special case of numeric\_limits<T>::min(), by evaluating the bit pattern as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{55   \textcolor{comment}{// a signed integer value. If it is the overflow case, we end up subtracting}}
\DoxyCodeLine{56   \textcolor{comment}{// one from the unsigned result, thus saturating to numeric\_limits<T>::max().}}
